SELECT * , b.name AS branch_name , c.para_name AS sex_name , d.para_name AS status_name FROM T_Cm_Emp a LEFT JOIN dbo.T_Cm_Branch b ON a.branch_id = b.id LEFT JOIN dbo.T_Cm_Code c ON c.para_value = a.sex_ind AND c.para_type = 'sex' LEFT JOIN dbo.T_Cm_Code d ON d.para_value = a.status AND d.para_type = 'office_statue'

SELECT a.* , b.link_name , b.link_address , b.link_telephone , b.link_mobilephone , b.link_area , b.link_memo, f.para_name AS creditlevel_name FROM T_Cm_Servicer a LEFT JOIN dbo.T_Cm_Link b ON a.link_id = b.id LEFT JOIN dbo.T_Cm_Code f ON f.para_value = a.credit_level AND para_type = 'customer_credit'
